  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_197dda61-7e6f-46ef-9b25-22c22bb49a2a'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

The friendships they've formed, the new family they've found, and the history they've forged will all play a part in helping them navigate the turbulent waters of the band's exploding popularity. A greedy executive hell-bent on success, a declining pop star looking for an edge, and a media circus that twists lies into truths are just some of the obstacles the lovers will have to overcome if they are going to remain together. Fame comes with a price-but will it cost Kiera and Kellan everything?</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/312954263" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/312954263?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=6-star-books">6-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer312954263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17432674042239501332"><b> FULL SPOILER-FREE REVIEW IS UP NOW!!! </b><br/><br/>And, first off, I am officially casting this guy as Kellan Kyle!! <br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380362960i/714168._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> 6 HUGE STARS!!! </b><br/><br/>WOW!!! I can’t breathe. Can’t think. <b> Reckless just blew me away! </b><br/><br/><b> It was <u> BRILLIANT </u> !!! An utterly delicious, addictive, angst-filled, heart-felt EPIC rockstar romance! </b><br/><br/>I swooned, I laughed, cried tears of happiness and tears of angst, my heart raced, was tied up in knots and, at times, just stopped entirely. I truly can’t say enough good about it.<br/><br/>I could NOT put this book </span>
  <span id="freeText17432674042239501332" style="display:none"><b> FULL SPOILER-FREE REVIEW IS UP NOW!!! </b><br><br>And, first off, I am officially casting this guy as Kellan Kyle!! <br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380362960i/714168._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 6 HUGE STARS!!! </b><br><br>WOW!!! I can’t breathe. Can’t think. <b> Reckless just blew me away! </b><br><br><b> It was <u> BRILLIANT </u> !!! An utterly delicious, addictive, angst-filled, heart-felt EPIC rockstar romance! </b><br><br>I swooned, I laughed, cried tears of happiness and tears of angst, my heart raced, was tied up in knots and, at times, just stopped entirely. I truly can’t say enough good about it.<br><br>I could NOT put this book down. I read it in one sitting staying up through the night until I finished around 7AM. I couldn’t flip the pages fast enough. It was completely engaging. I felt like I didn’t even want to blink. Literally my world ceased to exist for the duration of the read.<br><br>Just as with the first two books, SC Stephens’ smooth flowing, utterly addictive writing style reaches right into your heart and wraps you up in the story. I was 150% invested in EVERYTHING that happened. Every single part of my heart was completely involved in the story. I was there. Right THERE. From the first page till the last. (and even now… I can’t let go yet. I’m still “there”)<br><br>Given the happy ending of Effortless, this book starts off with a blissfully peaceful, almost dreamy feel to it. After all the roller coaster they’d been through, it was so wonderful to see Kellan and Kiera have a moment to enjoy the happiness they so well deserved.<br><br>But the life of a Rockstar is neither smooth nor private and the road ahead of them was rocky and bumpy as the band skyrocketed to fame and got sucked into the scrutiny of the spotlight and the uglier side of the industry.<br><br><i> “Making an album, going on tour… am I making a mistake? … All I want is a quiet life with you,” he continued. “What I just signed up for… isn’t exactly a quiet life.” <br><br>Wondering how to comfort him – when I often thought the same thing – I reached up… “Kellan, your life will never be quiet, no matter what you do.” … I placed a hand on his chest and looked him square in the eye. </i> <i> <b> “You belong on a stage. Its what you were born to do.” </b></i> <br><br>I have to say that I’ve always understood where Kiera was coming from in book #1 even though I found it frustrating. I felt that she grew as a person in book #2, but it was in this book where I really felt her maturity hit home. Some of her decisions and actions were just SO self-less that I honestly found myself even thinking at time that, if I was in her shoes, I probably wouldn’t have been able to be as self-less and understanding as she was.<br><br>Kellan… well, Kellan Kyle was just perfect. Sex on a Stick, God’s Gift to Women… and also just one of those most lovable and swooniest guys you’ll ever read about whose back story and desire to be loved just made my heart ache for him. <b> He is easily one of the best book heroes EVER written. </b><br><br>As a couple, they still had their issues but they had gotten SO much stronger. They had been tested, they had made their mistakes, and they had learned their lessons. But now their new found strength was put to the very ultimate test as the pressures of fame and stardom came at them from every side. They had a lot working against them but… love conquers all, right?<br><br>I have to say though that, for me, the ANGST in this book topped both Thoughtless &amp; Effortless. No. Freaking. Joke. There was this one particular issue that spanned from about 29-37% that just made my heart sink, drop, stop.. seriously, I could BARELY handle it. Holy freaking fuck. It made me cry tears of angst. No book has EVER made me cry tears of angst before. I’ve cried tears of sadness, heartbreak, betrayal and more but crying just ‘cuz the angst was so strong that I could barely handle it was definitely a first!<br><br>But, to offset the heart-wrenching angst, the romance was also back in full swoony force. On more than one occasion, Kellan’s words and actions made my heart clench and just brought tears to my eyes. The depth of his love for Kiera just rolls right off the page. You feel it so strongly. And you know Kiera felt the same way.<br><br>Never once did I doubt their commitment to each other – no matter what they were put through.<br><br><i> <b> “I love you too, Kiera. Just you. You’re my always.” </b></i> <br><br>This book really makes you consider the price of fame. At what point do you say no? Where does the line get drawn? There were so many time where truly I was just ready to say fuck fame – it just wasn’t worth this all. The plot honestly pushed me to the very edge of my comfort limits and even a bit beyond. But I loved that they didn’t make the same mistakes twice. Lessons were learned. And that’s life, right?<br><br>I really have to commend Kiera on her whole attitude towards Kellan’s fame though. Seriously, she couldn’t possibly have been more supportive, more understanding. And my heart went right out to Kellan for trying with all of his heart to keep his girl’s heart safe while still following his dreams.<br><br><i> <b> “I will always love you, Kellan. Your heart is safe with me.” <br><br>Kellan pulled me into a hug and let out a long, shaky breath as he held me. “Promise?” he whispered.<br><br>I squeezed him just a little bit tighter. “I promise.” </b></i> <br><br>To soothe your worried hearts, I’ll say that I honestly never once actually worried for their relationship. It was what they had to go through that gutted me. This book is not about cheating or separation. Keira and Kellan spend the majority of it physically together in fact. What this book is about is testing the strength of their bond and the struggles of maintaining a relationship while under the spotlight.<br><br><i> “Never again. I don’t care what’s at stake. I don’t care who I have to let down. I won’t ever do that to you again. You… or me. I’m done playing their game.” </i> <br><br>I loved that this book took the time to also focus on the other relationships. Anna and Griffin get their fair share of page time as do the other band mates, but my favorite side story line was the one between Kellan and Denny. I don’t want to say anything specific about it ‘cuz those interactions are ones you should experience for yourself but twice they brought me to tears. I was SO impressed and happy with where SC Stephens took their story. Seriously, touched my heart right to the very core.<br><br>She also took the story to places I never thought she would.. I mean she took Kellan Kyle and she….. gah! ok – lips are sealed. But seriously, around 80% I just had this huge “Holy shit. That did NOT just happen!!” moment! Still – like I said, I loved every minute of it… even the moments that made my heart stop.<br><br>But I did read the final 15% with my heart just filled to bursting with happiness, and I this huge perpetual smile on my face with happy tears in my eyes.<br><br><i> <b> “I love you. I would do it all over again if I needed to. I’d go back to the beginning for you.” </b></i> <br><br>By the end, I felt elated. I was emotional but my heart was completely satisfied and I can assure you that the ending is just PERFECT!<br><br>And I officially have the world’s biggest book hang over. EVER.<br><br>There are so many INCREDIBLE moment, lines, and scenes from this book that will be forever imprinted on my mind. I was thinking about mentioning some here but instead I’m going to just encourage you all to go read this amazing story and discover them for yourself. I’ve been re-reading a few of them while putting this review together and now have tears in my eyes. Seriously - LOVE LOVE LOVE this book, this journey, these characters… this story raises the bar and is one that will stay in my heart forever.<br><br>I don’t pull out the 6 star rating very often but this whole series truly deserves it. Any story that can take over my life so completely and make me fall in love with the characters so strongly needs that extra star. Above and beyond. That’s where this book went.<br><br>♥<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375138i/729634._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These 2 banners are from SC Stephen's facebook wall:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375138i/729635._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375138i/729636._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How I see Kellan and Keira:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380362885i/714061.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>God. I really love this series. ♥♥<br><br>For more of my reviews, come visit my book blog at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/">http://aestasbookblog.com/</a><br><br>Or come join my FB group at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905">http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17432674042239501332" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

The magnetic panty melting sexiness that is Kellan Kyle.<br/><br/>Kellan<br/><br/><a href='http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/EMOTIONAL%20WORD%20GIFS%20PT2/tumblr_mhgw4cbVu91ri68muo1_400_zps67a20ef1.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><u>
  <b>My Casting</b>
</u><br/><br/><a href='http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/Final%20edited%20version%20pt2/milakunis_zps8a75567c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText13501403322788762851" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW<b> -mature content reader discretion is advised.</b><br>5 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: Contemporary Romance<br><b>SIDENOTE:</b> Do not read if you have not read books 1&amp;2<br><br>Whether you loved it or felt it came up short there is one thing you cannot deny. The magnetic panty melting sexiness that is Kellan Kyle.<br><br>Kellan<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/EMOTIONAL%20WORD%20GIFS%20PT2/tumblr_mhgw4cbVu91ri68muo1_400_zps67a20ef1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375136ra/729617.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mhgw4cbVu91ri68muo1_400_zps67a20ef1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/excited/tumblr_mi5xgpw46p1s2q4bno1_500_zps91bd5f93.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375136ra/729618.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mi5xgpw46p1s2q4bno1_500_zps91bd5f93.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>
  <b>My Casting</b>
</u><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/Final%20edited%20version%20pt2/milakunis_zps8a75567c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375136i/729619.jpg" alt=" photo milakunis_zps8a75567c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/Final%20edited%20version%20pt2/LUCASBERNARDINI_zps19b50229.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375136i/729620.jpg" alt=" photo LUCASBERNARDINI_zps19b50229.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Used%20pt%203%20for%20book%20reviews/LUCASBERNARDINI1_zps4ffaff03.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375136i/729621.jpg" alt=" photo LUCASBERNARDINI1_zps4ffaff03.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Used%20pt%203%20for%20book%20reviews/LUCASBERNARDINI2_zpsa5c809cd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375136i/729622.jpg" alt=" photo LUCASBERNARDINI2_zpsa5c809cd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I...<br><br>Shit...<br><br>I don't even know where to begin. I'll just talk about what I loved! <br><br>One of the most highly anticipated books of 2013 had it's highs and lows for the characters we have grown to love.. And I enjoyed every second of it. Maybe it's just me but I love how relationships are captured in this book.<br><br><b>Kiera and Kellan</b><br><br>These two ripped out my heart, lungs, liver and all other vital organs throughout this whole series.<br><br>In Thoughtless<br>I loved him and hated her<br><br>In Effortless<br>I loved him and slowly started to like her<br><br>In Reckless<br>I loved him and I totally have a girl crush on her *shrugs* What can I say, she grew on me! <br><br>Yeah, she made some bad judgement calls but overall my girl held it <b>DOWN</b> for her man. And that put a smile on my face. She went to bat for her relationship when all arrows pointed to failuresville.(Yeah, I made that word up.)*shrugs*<br><br> <b>'. . . my heart was anchored to Kellan. Being apart from him stretched my soul in opposite directions. It was painful. No, it was torture. He was everything to me, and I didn’t want to miss a moment of his journey just because parts of it were unpleasant.'</b><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/prettygal_zpsa079e00c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375136ra/729623.gif" alt=" photo prettygal_zpsa079e00c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I take it alllll back.. I considered Kiera weak for some of the things that happened in Thoughtless but in Reckless she proved that she is no weakling. She had to bare some things I don't think I would have endured. Which goes to show you really should never judge a person.<br><br><b>
  <i><br>“I don’t want to hurt you. And I don’t see how any of this won’t hurt you.”</i>
</b><br> Pulling back from him, I said,<br><br><b>
  <i> “And I don’t want you to give up on your dream because of me.”</i>
</b> ~Kellan and Kiera<br><br><br>Kiera and Kellan are a team whatever they face they always faced it together head on and I think that is the ONLY reason they have survived.<br><br><br>I love and appreciated how S.C. Stephens highlighted all the characters and of course there is always one who stands out. Griffin.<br><br><b>'Griffin had impregnated my sister. He really was family now. Lord help me.'</b> ~Kiera<br><br><b>Griffin and Anna</b><br>In all his male egotistical driven macho raunchy glory Griffin stole the show. We really get a glimpse at the man behind the over the top raunchy comments. While I still question Griffin's capability to be a father(because honestly should this guy be allowed to teach another human being anything???) Exactly. I no longer question his love for Anna. He admitted out of his own potty mouth...<br><br><i>
  <b>“You’re in love with me?”</b>
</i><br> Every head shifted to the open hotel room door that Anna was leaning against. The energy in the air shifted again as Griffin locked eyes with her. Matt and Evan released him as he whispered, <br><i>
  <b>“Yes.”</b>
</i><br><br>Other relationships are briefly shown with the other two band mates. But the relationship that really <b>really</b> did a number on me was the one between Kellan, Kiera and Denny. The mutual love and respect tugged at my heartstrings.<br>And I won't dwell on it since I don't want to spoil it, however I will say that <b>I LOVE ME SOME DENNY!!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/excited/hearts_zps2cbeef3d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375136ra/729624.gif" alt=" photo hearts_zps2cbeef3d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now as I previously mentioned I enjoyed these characters but there were a few rotten apples in the bunch. Sienna and Nick. In fact I have a special message for Sienna check it out<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/tumblr_mgyc1411La1ql5yr7o1_400_zps7d72d164.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375136ra/729625.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mgyc1411La1ql5yr7o1_400_zps7d72d164.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_346274042" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/346274042" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/346274042?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476718200" href="/book/show/15851738-reckless">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer346274042" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1472796209083228532"><b>
  <i>“I love you. I would do it all over again if I needed to. I’d go back to the beginning for you.”~ Kellan</i>
</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380440i/737339._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Reckless read like one enormous epilogue to me and I thought that it was ABSOLUTE PERFECTION! <br/> <br/>Does this book have an excess amount of angst or drama? No, but it gives KK lovers their happily ever after and I’ve been on book hangover ever since!<br/><br/>S.C. Stephens engrossing writing completely captured me from the first book of the series to the last line of Reckless. A reader can’t help fallin</span>
  <span id="freeText1472796209083228532" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“I love you. I would do it all over again if I needed to. I’d go back to the beginning for you.”~ Kellan</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380440i/737339._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reckless read like one enormous epilogue to me and I thought that it was ABSOLUTE PERFECTION! <br> <br>Does this book have an excess amount of angst or drama? No, but it gives KK lovers their happily ever after and I’ve been on book hangover ever since!<br><br>S.C. Stephens engrossing writing completely captured me from the first book of the series to the last line of Reckless. A reader can’t help falling in love with Kellan Kyle. There is no way of getting around it nor would a reader look for one...just see my name above.<br><br>I didn’t agree with how Kiera handled her situation in Thoughtless. I loved how she grew through the sequel Effortless and by the time I finished Reckless, I was so pleased how she grew from a girl into the woman that I knew she could be. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I’d always hoped that the man I married would love me beyond reason but Kellan…loved me beyond anything.”~ Kiera</i>
</b><br><br><i></i>P.S. I’m anxiously awaiting the release of Irresistible! Can I get an advanced reading copy of her future books?<br><br>Reckless brought great success for the D-Bags. Kiera was supportive of Kellan and the boys throughout this book. Some tried to break them up or capitalize on Kellan but the couple stuck together and they only got stronger. NO ONE could stand between them or break them up and believe me Siera Sexton and Joey tried.<br> <br>Kellan Kyle is the best book male character of all time PERIOD! He’s sex on a stick (Cowboy Kellan...HOT) he will sing you to sleep, he will write you love notes and he will love you so fiercely and completely that everything else in the word pales in comparison.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Us against the world? That sounds like wonderful odds.” ~Kellan </i>
</b><br><br>All of the characters, Denny, Abby, Griffin, Anna, Evan, Matt, Jenny and Rachel grow throughout this series. It happens before our eyes I really feel like they are my friends too. <br> <br>Time heals all wounds and thankfully, the love triangle of Thoughtless has moved past the betrayal and hurt to a good place.<br><br><b>
  <i>”We all laughed, and I marveled at how far we’d all come. We were so different from the people we were when we’d all started living together—stronger, more confident, more secure in ourselves. And yet, we were still exactly the same. We cared about each other. We supported each other. We looked out for each other. And now that the sting of betrayal and guilt was only a dull ache in the background, the three of us were what I’d always hoped we would be—the best of friends.”~ Kiera</i>
</b><br><br>To all those romance fans this series had it all! Looking back at the journey, I’m so happy how the story played out, but I’m sad that it’s ended. Thankfully, a reread will do the trick. <br> <br><b>
  <i>”Passion, friendship, love, loyalty, trust...if you found the right person...you really could have it all.” ~ Kiera </i>
</b><br><br>I truly believe that somewhere out there in Seattle, sitting at their table at Pete’s Bar, the gang is getting together to reminisce over a beer. Save a seat for me!!<br><br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="1472796209083228532" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer375057311" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8422274422280801345">Anyone else worried about the title of the book.....Reckless. I am not sure if I can handle a disappointment, I want to believe in their story but he is going on tour again with all those girls. I think my stomach hurts right now. I wouldn't be as worried if I never read the original endng to Thoughtless but after reading it I know the author has it in her for a sad outcome. Keeping my fingers crossed cause I really like these two characters, well I like Keira but LOVE Kellan. Here's the link to</span>
  <span id="freeText8422274422280801345" style="display:none">Anyone else worried about the title of the book.....Reckless. I am not sure if I can handle a disappointment, I want to believe in their story but he is going on tour again with all those girls. I think my stomach hurts right now. I wouldn't be as worried if I never read the original endng to Thoughtless but after reading it I know the author has it in her for a sad outcome. Keeping my fingers crossed cause I really like these two characters, well I like Keira but LOVE Kellan. Here's the link to the original ending of Thoughtless:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.fictionpress.com/s/2715147/1/Thoughtless-Original-Ending">http://www.fictionpress.com/s/2715147...</a><br /><br /><br />Updated:<br />I'm so sad, I can't believe it's over and their story is done. I love Kellan so much it is borderline crazy. I loved how these characters grew in the trilogy. In Thoughtless I wanted to smack Kierra at times even though I could relate to her I still wanted to slap her (probably because I love Kellan so). In Effortless it was painful at times reading their pain and having trust issues. There were times I thought maybe they could never fully trust. But Reckless they are both stronger in their relationship. That's why it was painful to read. I could feel their pain at the choices the label was making and Sienna.....well she's a bitch troll. The angst was there and my stomach hurt from the beginning. I did think the story dipped a little about 40% in, but it did recover. Remembering the original ending to Thoughtless I was holding my breath at times nearing the last 1/3 of the story. In the end, I was proud of Kellan and Kierra, their relationship evolved and I'm glad I got to witness the transformation. In fact all the D-Bags and company grew up and I was happy for them. (Especially Griffin) This has been one of my favorite series. Thank you SC Stephens for this story. I felt so juvenile at times being so worried about a book (hence the above review before Rekless was released). That just goes to show what a great story these books were. Seriously though, can Kellan Kyle be any more perfect and sweet....did I mention how much I love him.....well it's worth mentioning again "KELLAN KYLE IS A ROCK GOD"</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer410868241" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1146449532724083750"><b>4 1/2 Shining Stars!</b><br/><br/><b>OKAY, I'm eating humble pie!</b> I wasn't planning to read this book because I was disappointed in the last one; however, my curiosity got the better me, and what a surprise...this book was TERRIFIC! <br/><br/>Unlike the second book, this one, for me, made sense. I felt Kellan and Kiera were true to their characters, to their past experiences, and to their relationship. This plot was true-to-life and it was refreshing to see two characters already in love working together to keep and maint</span>
  <span id="freeText1146449532724083750" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2 Shining Stars!</b><br /><br /><b>OKAY, I'm eating humble pie!</b> I wasn't planning to read this book because I was disappointed in the last one; however, my curiosity got the better me, and what a surprise...this book was TERRIFIC! <br /><br />Unlike the second book, this one, for me, made sense. I felt Kellan and Kiera were true to their characters, to their past experiences, and to their relationship. This plot was true-to-life and it was refreshing to see two characters already in love working together to keep and maintain their relationship against real-world challenges. My heart broke for them as they battled the insidious environment of the music industry and the injustices heaped upon them. My heart rejoiced for them, however, as they fought tooth-and-nail to preserve their relationship and their love for each other. <br /><br />In this book Keira's strength of character shined brilliantly, and Kellan...was...well...Kellan...swoon-worthy and perfectly delectable. What can I say...I just loved them! I'm so glad I read this book. <b>Humble pie never tasted so great!!</b><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>September 9, 2012 original post</u>
</b><br /><br />Can someone please tell me how a book that isn't due for release UNTIL March 5, 2013, and is still currently being written, already has 175 <i>ratings</i>?<br /><br />From what S.C. Stephen's September 3rd, 2012 <a href="http://m.facebook.com/note.php?note_id=283581171720414" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> update says, she is STILL currently writing this book. You wouldn't know that, however, by the amount of readers who have <i>already</i> rated this unfinished book. Unbelievable!!!<br /><br /><b>As of today, September 9, 2012, there are:<br /><br />5 star ratings: 137 <br />4 star ratings: 20<br />3 star ratings: 4<br />2 star ratings: 2<br />1 star ratings: 6</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1146449532724083750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/312203244" />
    <a title="Natalie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4676969-natalie"><img alt="Natalie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551820942p2/4676969.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/312203244?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie" href="/user/show/4676969-natalie">Natalie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19018152-reckless">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer312203244" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2279974029044417852"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386247443i/7320237.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️ ! Life in the spotlight proves more challenging than expected for Kelly and Kiera. Will love survive or will fame tear them apart?</b><br/><br/> Oh my god you guys!!! I think that for the first time that the last(!) book in a series may just be my favourite! ”Reckless” was just <u>SO</u> good!! Any new book release has yet to make me so excited that I was for “Reckless'.” Right in that moment, I felt that “Reckless” was the book I've been waiting my entire life to read. “Reckless” continues right where “Eff</span>
  <span id="freeText2279974029044417852" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386247443i/7320237.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️ ! Life in the spotlight proves more challenging than expected for Kelly and Kiera. Will love survive or will fame tear them apart?</b><br><br> Oh my god you guys!!! I think that for the first time that the last(!) book in a series may just be my favourite! ”Reckless” was just <u>SO</u> good!! Any new book release has yet to make me so excited that I was for “Reckless'.” Right in that moment, I felt that “Reckless” was the book I've been waiting my entire life to read. “Reckless” continues right where “Effortless” ended. Kellan and Kiera are now married in 'spirit' and they have never been happier or been in a better place in their relationship. But drama awaits them tight around the corner in form of Kellans ex-roommate Joey and a sex tape. Soon it's also time for Kiera to join Kellan on tour, something not without its challenges. Now when D-bags finally has hit it big, everyone seems to want a piece of the cake. And Kellan. Poor Kiera, it's not always easy to be married to the worlds sexiest rockstar and be hated by all female population.<br><br>Needless to say that I loved this book over and beyond. It's been years since the release and I can't tell you how many times I reread it. Seriously, I can't. I've said it before and I'm saying it again; THIS SERIES HAS TAKEN OVER MY WORD. Every time I read these books something magical happens; it's like a vacation from the world and nothing no longer exists, except for Kellan. Kellan and Kiera really is two awesome characters that never get old. I could read about them forefeet. OMG; especially Kellan!' Who isn't madly in love with him? Raise a hand. He's completely irresistible.<br><br>“Reckless” continues to be one of my very favourite books ever and the biggest reason is and always will be KELLAN! But let's not forget all the other AWESOME characters; every member in D-bags, Denny, Kiera's sister Anna, Denny and of course Kiera herself. I would read a book about each character but Kellan is definitely the shiny star everyone wants to read about. The locations for this book took my breath away and into my own, personal reading heaven; Los Angeles and a filthy rich, luxuries lifestyle and on the tour bus with Kellan, Griff &amp; co. LOVE !!! Three books aren't enough, I need more of my Kellan fix, I'm already going through serious withdrawals. Kellan and Kiera will forever be one of my top couples, if not my number one top couple. And Kellan...you'll always be the love of my life. 4.5 stars.<br><br><b>| Hero |</b> 5 | <b>| Angst |</b> Medium focus |<br><b>| Heroine |</b> 5 | <b>| Romance |</b> | High focus |<br><b>| Sexual tension |</b> 5 | <b> | Suspense |</b> Low focus |<br><b>| Storytelling |</b> 5 | <b> | Humour |</b> Medium focus |<br><b>| Plot |</b> 5 | <b> | Darkness | </b> Low focus |<br><b>| Story ending |</b> 5 | </span>

<div id="review_444132373" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/444132373" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/444132373?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=need-it-in-paperback">need-it-in-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=five-plus-stars">five-plus-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=rock-star-hero">rock-star-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer444132373" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10090145861102612462"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395845i/762594._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395845i/762595._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh my God! I feel like I've waited so long for this book and it did <i>not</i> disappoint! I read <i>Thoughtless</i> and <i>Effortless</i> before I ever started blogging, so I'm a little nervous to write this review... here's why...<br/><br/>I could read about Kellan and Kiera forever. In fact, I wish it were a never ending book soap opera that was drip fed to us week by week so that I could keep up with their lives! I feel like I know them so well and it makes my heart ache when I remind myself 'These are not real people!'<br/><br/>I </span>
  <span id="freeText10090145861102612462" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395845i/762594._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395845i/762595._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh my God! I feel like I've waited so long for this book and it did <i>not</i> disappoint! I read <i>Thoughtless</i> and <i>Effortless</i> before I ever started blogging, so I'm a little nervous to write this review... here's why...<br><br>I could read about Kellan and Kiera forever. In fact, I wish it were a never ending book soap opera that was drip fed to us week by week so that I could keep up with their lives! I feel like I know them so well and it makes my heart ache when I remind myself 'These are not real people!'<br><br>I want to know how many beautiful babies they make. I want to know how the D-Bags' career pans out. I want to know what they do for the holidays... Every. Single. Year! I don't want their story to ever end. And now it has. And now I'm sad and feeling a little lost.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Everyone eventually falls for the two of you together. You're meant to be."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>No review I write is going to do this story justice. The Thoughtless series changed reading for me. Fifty Shades got me back into reading... it reminded me that I needed to make the time to read again. And I thought that I'd never recover from Christian Grey... I went on to read Love Unrehearsed, and fell in love with Ryan. I read Beautiful Disaster and fell in love with Travis... And then there was Thoughtless. And Kellan Kyle!!! <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Kellan Kyle, you are the love of my life. You have my heart from now until the end of forever."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And nothing will ever top him. <br><br>I can't tell you what it is about S.C. Stephens' characters that have me hook, line and sinker. There are a whole host of hot, sexy, badass, gorgeous book boyfriends out there... but Kellan has my heart over all of them and I think he always will.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Whatever happens from here on out, I want you to know that I don't regret anything. Being with you, loving you, experiencing this with you... it's all been worth it, and we'll get through this together. We're a team. It's us against the world."<br>"Us against the world? That sounds like wonderful odds."<br>"It's better than no odds at all."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I feel a little in mourning right now, knowing that this series has finally come to an end, after so much waiting, so much hype and so much adoration. But for me, it will always be the series that reminds me just <i>why</i> I love reading. It captures me and it pulls me into another world. I adore every single character, even Kiera, who made me so mad in the beginning. And even Griffin, who completely grossed me out.<br><br>I want to be friends with Anna, Jenny, Rachel and Kate. I want my man to be friends with the D-Bags. I want a rock like Denny in my life. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I knew going into this that a story about us was also going to be a story about the two of you. And it should be. He was a big part of your life, and I'm okay with your history. It made you who you are. And I happen to be in love with who you are."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And I don't think I even need to mention the fact that I want to date/live with/kiss/lick/have babies with/marry Kellan Friggin' Kyle!!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Our lives are crazy. When moments to remember happen, you have to pause a second to appreciate them. Otherwise none of this is worth it. And getting married to you is definitely a moment to remember."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Errr... and can I just mention... there is an incredibly sexy scene with a stripping half naked cowboy. *fans self* Oh. My. God! I need me one of those!<br><br>As for my casting pictures... there is only one person that I could ever cast as Kellan. I know everybody has their own ideas, but the Efron has always been my KK. Has been since the first image of him singing on stage with those gorgeous blue eyes and that sexy brown bed hair.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I didn't think it was possible, but I'm pretty sure I love you even more. How you see me... I never thought anyone would ever..."<br>"That's because you don't see yourself as clearly as I see you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm not going to write too much more. a) I think I've gushed enough and b) I don't want to spoil anything for anybody. I know that <i>Thoughtless</i> isn't everybodies cup of tea. I know some people hate the cheating element. But, I'll say it again, this series stole my heart. I ate up every word and then read at snails pace towards the end of <i>Reckless</i>, trying to stop it from ending. So, if you haven't read this yet... firstly, have you been hiding under a rock... and secondly, I strongly suggest you jump to it already. And if you hate it and wish I'd never recommended it to you... please don't tell me. ;) It'd be like insulting my best friend or my child. I love it that much and I won't be held responsible for my actions.<br><br>Right, I'm going to go now. I'm going to go and dream about Kellan and wallow in the tragedy that KK doesn't actually exist. God, it's worse than knowing Santa isn't real. S.C. Stephens, I hope you know, you are responsible for many a forlorn woman and many a too high expectation.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>You'll never know how incredible you are to me, how desperately I love you. I would do it all over again if I needed to. I'd go back to the beginning for you.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395845i/762596._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389731917i/8051686._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389731917i/8051687._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389731917i/8051688._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389731917i/8051689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Smittens-Book-Blog/525405204177978">http://www.facebook.com/pages/Smitten...</a></span>

<div id="review_450831372" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/450831372" />
    <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty"><img alt="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481371426p2/13273769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/450831372?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2012</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer450831372" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8070764877307016120"><b> INFINITE STARS!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>My Kellan...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786198i/480018.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>With Keira...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379789225i/519961._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Words cannot describe how much I LOVE this series... I've waited for months for this book, and it was more than I ever expected, I was dying to find out what happened but I never wanted it to end!. S.C. Stephans did us <u>ALL </u>proud and I will forever be grateful to her for bringing Kellen Kyle into my life...<br/><br/>My Heart is Broken that this is over... But then I think...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765380.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the first two books we joined Keira and Kellan in their incredible Journey finding lo</span>
  <span id="freeText8070764877307016120" style="display:none"><b> INFINITE STARS!!!!!!</b><br><br>My Kellan...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786198i/480018.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With Keira...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379789225i/519961._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Words cannot describe how much I LOVE this series... I've waited for months for this book, and it was more than I ever expected, I was dying to find out what happened but I never wanted it to end!. S.C. Stephans did us <u>ALL </u>proud and I will forever be grateful to her for bringing Kellen Kyle into my life...<br><br>My Heart is Broken that this is over... But then I think...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765380.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the first two books we joined Keira and Kellan in their incredible Journey finding love and success...<br><br><b>We lived through them...<br>Laughed with them<br>Had fun with them..<br>Felt their pain..<br>Felt their weakness <br>Felt their passion..<br>And last shared their happiness..</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765381.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Tangling my hands through his hair, I gazed at him until I thought my heart might burst. He unwaveringly met my eyes. “I love you too, Kiera. Just you. You’re my always.”"</b><br><br>This book is the ultimate test on the love of Keira and Kellan and picks up from Effortless..<br><br>The D-Bags are on their tour and Keira is joining Kellan soon in LA to go touring with him..<br>When she finally gets there, Kellan proposes to her in a room filled with Rose petals..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765382._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Once on tour they are introduced to extremely famous Sienna Sexton- she is beautiful and sexy and also a singer.<br>Kellan and his band are given an offer to do a collaboration with her.<br>Sienna basically puts Kellans name out there with their song and speculation that Kellan and Sienna are a couple. His greedy executive pushes him to do all the things his not happy with.<br>They have to make a music video together.. A sexy video...<br><br><b> Kellan Kyle - My boyfriend the Rock Star!! : D</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765383.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b> WELL DONE Keira!! YOU MADE ME SO PROUD</b>
</i><br><br>Keira has grown soooo much from Thoughtless/Effortless.. She is not whiney or irritating or doubting herself. She never holds Kellan back in his career. Always encouraging him to do things even if its not comfortable for her.. <br><br><b>Kellan is a star and he was always meant to shine...</b><br><br>Stirring false rumors Sienna causes a frenzy with their 'relationship' then a sex video emerges and people claim it's Sienna with Kellan. <br>Throughout all of this Keira stands by him.. In their secret 'bubble' they can be alone...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765384.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I Lovvvve all the details in this book, it was the first time in a long time I didn't think the story was rushed. The love and passion between these two is amazing!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765385.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Kellan throws a surprise bachelorette party for Keira. I love how he always does the sweetest things..<br><b> "Our lives are crazy. When moments to remember happen, you have to pause a second to appreciate them. Otherwise none of this”—he indicted the bus—“is worth it. And getting married to you is definitely a moment to remember.”"</b><br><br>Again their love is tested.. Paparazzi see Kellan and Keira together.. This throws the media into another crazy frenzy. Fans think his cheating on Sienna.<br><br>They make a vow to each other...<br><br><b>"Whatever happens from here on out, I want you to know that I don’t regret anything. Being with you, loving you, experiencing this with you . . . it’s all been worth it, and we’ll get through this together.” I smiled. “We’re a team. It’s us against the world.”"</b><br><br>They come clean to the world.. On national radio.. People ridicule Keira as she is 'the other woman'- Kellan wants the truth out there... The truth will set them free... Unfortunately tragedy happens and the press/fans and photographers hound Kellan and Keira.<br>Keira is pushed to the street where a truck is going to hit her but Kellan runs and pulls her away but gets badly hurt in the process. <br><br><b>I WAS LIKE....</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765386.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In hospital family and friends come... Kellan sees his fans praying for him.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kellen and Keira get married... In hospital.. And it's soo perfect! <br><br><b> "Kiera Michelle Allen, my life was empty before you stepped into it. I thought I had everything I needed, but only because I didn’t let myself want anything. And then I saw you, and you burned a hole straight through me. I have never wanted anything more in my life. And I have never been more terrified in all my life. In all my life,” he repeated."<br>"And then, beyond some miracle that I’ll never understand, I got to keep you, and now . . . I’m only just beginning to understand what it means to truly want something. Because I want so much now. I want to make you happy. I want to give you the world. I want you to be proud of me. I want to comfort you. I want you to comfort me. I want to hold you when you’re scared. I want you to hold me when I’m scared. I want to make you laugh. I want to make you blush.” Leaning in, he whispered, “I want to make you scream.”"<br>"“I want to give you a home. I want to fill it with children. I want to take care of you. I want to grow old with you. I want you by my side, every day.” Folding his hand over mine once my ring was in place, he shrugged and shook his head. “I just want you. Do you want me too?”"- Kellan</b><br><br><b>"I never thought of myself as anything but plain and ordinary until you came along. The way you look at me, the way you see me . . . you pull something out of me. When I want to hide, you urge me forward. When I think I’m not good enough, you make me believe I am. When I feel anything but pretty, you convince me I’m beautiful. Just being around you makes me feel special. You don’t think you’re good at loving people, but you are. Your friends, your family . . . the level of love that you have for people astounds me. You don’t think people love you back, but they do. They fiercely love you. I fiercely love you. I’ve never met anyone as passionate as you, as kindhearted as you . . . as amazing as you. You love with every fiber of your soul. You inspire me every day. And if you’ll agree to be my husband, I’ll do my best to make you proud of me, to inspire you.”"-Keira </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765387.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>"You’ll never know how incredible you are to me, how desperately I love you. I would do it all over again if I needed to. I’d go back to the beginning for you."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396873i/765388.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Passion, friendship, love, loyalty, trust . . . if you found the right person . . . you really could have it all."</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The D-Bags go on another tour, they are international stars and they win a Grammy!<br>Keira is pregnant and they have a baby boy named Ryder.<br>And are deeply in love as they always were... <br><br>We get to interact not only with the loving Kellan but with other band members and Crazy ass Griffin, a very pregnant Anna and Denny.. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Kellan Kyle is one of those characters who will stay in your heart forever... Atleast I know he will always be in mine... &lt;3 &lt;3</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer383462613" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8628766503212256074"><b>5 Kellan loving stars!!!!!</b><br/><br/>Reckless exceeded all my expectations! Absolutely loved it!!! <br/><br/><b>
  <i>You’ll never know how incredible you are to me , how desperately I love you. I would do it all over again if I needed to. I’d go back to the beginning for you.</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>KELLAN KYLE</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/476cf411-7672-450c-b70b-ab0a378a6928_zpscc62d12f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><b>“Sex on a stick.”</b> <br/><br/><b>KIERA ALLEN</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/2383f380-08b5-44b9-ad4a-e427d6a62def_zps442396c0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386344i/745796.jpg' alt=' photo 2383f380-08b5-44b9-ad4a-e427d6a62def_zps442396c0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> KELLAN <3 KIERA </b><br/><b>
  <i>“Everyone eventually falls for the two of you together. You’re meant to be.”</i>
</b> <a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/b545170d-ce6e-4d25-80a2-2da5c60f8a9b_zps21005d10.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386344i/745797._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo b545170d-ce6e-4d25-80a2-2da5c60f8a9b_zps21005d10.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>I would always be first in his eyes. We were a good match. A perfect match. Soul mates.</i>
</b> <br/><br/><br/>Reckles</span>
  <span id="freeText8628766503212256074" style="display:none"><b>5 Kellan loving stars!!!!!</b><br><br>Reckless exceeded all my expectations! Absolutely loved it!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>You’ll never know how incredible you are to me , how desperately I love you. I would do it all over again if I needed to. I’d go back to the beginning for you.</i>
</b><br><br><b>KELLAN KYLE</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/476cf411-7672-450c-b70b-ab0a378a6928_zpscc62d12f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386344i/745795._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 476cf411-7672-450c-b70b-ab0a378a6928_zpscc62d12f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>“Sex on a stick.”</b> <br><br><b>KIERA ALLEN</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/2383f380-08b5-44b9-ad4a-e427d6a62def_zps442396c0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386344i/745796.jpg" alt=" photo 2383f380-08b5-44b9-ad4a-e427d6a62def_zps442396c0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> KELLAN &lt;3 KIERA </b><br><b>
  <i>“Everyone eventually falls for the two of you together. You’re meant to be.”</i>
</b> <a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/b545170d-ce6e-4d25-80a2-2da5c60f8a9b_zps21005d10.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386344i/745797._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo b545170d-ce6e-4d25-80a2-2da5c60f8a9b_zps21005d10.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>I would always be first in his eyes. We were a good match. A perfect match. Soul mates.</i>
</b> <br><br><br>Reckless picked up right where Effortless left off. The D-bags got a record deal and they are going on tour. Kiera and Kellan are together and stronger than ever. Completely committed to one another. Kiera has just graduated college and is going on tour with the boys. There is a lot of pressure coming in all directions, many obstacles are thrown there way, will their love be able to withstand it all??? <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e643f71e-e962-44d7-921c-ae086f25a7f0_zps9aa1c6bd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386344i/745798.jpg" alt=" photo e643f71e-e962-44d7-921c-ae086f25a7f0_zps9aa1c6bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I will ALWAYS love Kellan Kyle. He is near perfect to me. If it is possible, he may have been even MORE perfect in this book.... swoon! <br><b>
  <i>There were points where I had been whiny, clingy, petty, wishy-washy... downright annoying.</i>
</b><br>Yes Kiera, you were.... but a very pleasant surprise... Kiera didn’t annoy me in this book at all! Yay! I like Kiera, but in the first two books, there were times she drove me crazy! Glad she had it together in this one. <br>Sienna.... I have a few choice words for that one. And reading the music video scene made me sick to my stomach. I actually had to stop reading for a few minutes... Ugh. <br>Griffin was as hilarious as ever. I loved how he evolved in this book, but still managed to stay his crazy self! My favorite Griffin quote: <b>
  <i>“You should have heard him complaining in wardrobe. Oh, poor me, I have to go make out with a hot superstar. Woman fawn over me where ever I go. I have fucktastic hair and an eight pack. Boo-hoo.”</i>
</b><br>And Denny... I have always been Team Kellan 100% But I still have a soft spot for Denny, always have. There was one part of the book with him that really touched me, had me it tears... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[At the hospital when he tells Kellan “I know we’ve put the past behind us, and I know we’re friends, but I want you to know, without a doubt in your head, that we’re still brothers. You understand me?” <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br> Overall a FANTASTIC READ!!!! Such a great book ... and for those of you wondering.... the ending/epilogue was PERFECTION!!!!!<br><br><b>Passion, friendship, love, loyalty, trust..... if you found the right person... you really could have it all.</b><br><br>I will leave you with this... <br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/8157c770-6ee8-4543-8346-d1fa70e97343_zps460c4740.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386344i/745799.jpg" alt=" photo 8157c770-6ee8-4543-8346-d1fa70e97343_zps460c4740.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
